Thou art become hot; made to be hot; for the hot thee; for the hot ones thee."16 Then he says, тАЬO Hotr╠е do you recite what you have to." Having taken hold of him and standing, he says, “The oblation is boiled.” Having crossed beyond and having caused to announce, he says (to the Hotr╠е), “Do you recite the y─Бjy─Б for the offering of Dadhigharma.тАЭ

English

A piece of gold is tied to the last fringe of this piece of cloth. Having taken this up, he says, “Come O sacrificer.” Having gone around along the north of the ─Аgn─лdhr─лya mound and along the north of the Sadas and having led him into the (Pragvaс╣Б┼Ыa) shed, while his near relations have contacted successively and have been covered under a canopy, having melted clarified butter over the G─Бrhapatya, having taken four spoonfuls into the ladle, having caught the end of the piece of cloth on the handle of the ladle, he makes offerings on the G─Бrhapatya with two verses addressed to S┼лrya, “Thy rays bear upwards god S┼лrya, the lord of wealth, so that every thing may be visible, Sv─Бh─Б.”23 Having taken up another four spoonfuls, he makes an offering on the G─Бrhapatya itself with the verse, “The bright face of the gods has arisen, the eye of Mitra, Varuс╣Зa and Agni. It has filled in the heaven, the earth and midregion, the sun, the soul of the moving and the standing, Sv─Бh─Б.”23 Having hastened to the ─Аgn─лdhra fire, having taken up four spoonfuls into the ladle, having caught the end of the piece of cloth on the handle of the ladle, he makes an offering on the ─Аgn─лdhra fire with the verse containing the word naya. тАЬO Agni, lead us by a fair path to wealth, O god, knowing all the ways, drive from us the sin that leads astray. We shall pay deep homage to thee, Sv─Бh─Б.”24 Having made the offering, he takes up the piece of gold with the formula, тАЬDo thou go to the heaven; fly towards the sun."23

English

Going around by the right, (the sacrificer) approaches them with the formula, тАЬI reach your form with (my) form; your age with (my age)."25 He distributes them with the formula, “May Tutha, all-knowing, assign you in the highest firmament.”25 He comes towards the Sadas with the formula, “This gift of thine, O Agni, comes impelled by the Soma. Lead it by the path of Mitra. Do you go on by the path of the holy order, of brilliant gifts, leading prosperity by the path of sacrifice.”25

English

Having gone round along the west of the Havirdh─Бna shed88 and then along the south, having dug out by means of the wooden sword towards the south of M─Бrj─Бl─лya mound, having sprinkled water, and having strewn darbha-blades pointing towards the south, the sacrificer sprinkles on it with water with the formula, “May the fathers be cleansed, may the grand fathers be cleansed, may the great grandfathers be cleansed.” He gives three roasted grains with the formula, “This is thine O father N.N. and those that belong to thee; this is thine O grandfather N.N. and those that belong to thee, this is thine O great grandfather N.N. and those that belong to thee.”89 Having said, тАЬHere O fathers, rejoice here with your respective shares,тАЭ89 and having turned towards the north, he utters the Saс╕Нс╕Нhotr╠е formula.90

Having turned about, having similarly cleansed with water, and having come by the same route by which he had gone, he offers two spoonfuls on the ─Аgn─лdhr─лya fire with the two verses, “Whatever fault has been mine, Agni has set it right, all-knower, he who belongs to all men.”91 “Agni has given back the eye-sight; Indra and Br╠еhaspati have given it back. Do you two O A┼Ыvins, replace my eyesight within the eyes.тАЭ91

English

They offer splinters on the ─Аhavan─лya with the formula, “Thou art the expiation of the sin committed in respect of gods sv─Бh─Б; thou art the expiation of the sin committed in respect of man, sv─Бh─Б; thou art the expiation committed in respect of the fathers, sv─Бh─Б.”92 Having sat around the Soma mixed with water, they consume it by smelling with the formula, “O god Soma, I, having obtained consent, consume thee who art purified in water, who art pressed by man, over whom the yajus is uttered, for whom S─Бman is chanted and ┼Ъastra is recited, who art made by the fathers into food to win horses and cows and for whom consent has been obtained.”92 Having poured down the water and having stood up, they pray to ─Аditya:

“We have drunk Soma; we have become immortal; we have seen the light; we have attained the gods. What the evil spirit would do to us? What the injury perpetrated by man, O immortal Soma”?93

If the sun has already set, they pray to the ─Аhavan─лya with this verse. Having hastened to the ─Аgn─лdhra chamber, they consume the drops of curds with the verse, тАЬOf Dadhikr─Бvan have I sung, the swift strong horse. May he make our mouths fragrant; may he lengthen our lives.”94

The Adhvaryu, having turned by the right, having hastened to the west, having made the Patn─лsaс╣Бy─Бja offerings, having gone towards the east, having swollen the Dhruva ladle (with clarified butter), makes offerings with the six praising verses, “May Dhatr╠е the giver rejoice in this our offering; may Savitr╠е, may Praj─Бpati the lord of treasures, may Agni. O gods, carrying the oblations, do you proceed to the sun the resort of all and subsequently to the heaven.”93
